Page 8

Closure of the Tianjin Republic Daily

▲The North China Daily in Peiping Suffers the Same Destruction

Tianjin dispatch from the Central News Agency: The Tianjin Republic Daily, directly under the Central Propaganda Department, officially began publication on December 1st of last year. Its daily editorials and records were all devoted to upholding the Central Government and maintaining unity and peace. After Yan Xishan's telegrams were published, the newspaper upheld justice and criticized Yan's accusations. When telegrams from Shang Zhen, Lu Zhonglin, and others were released, clearly rebelling against the Central Government, the newspaper published forceful editorials against them, sparing no effort. As a result, it incurred the disfavor of the local military and political authorities in the city. On the afternoon of the 19th, at 1 PM, the city government sent a letter ordering Zhang Xiangding, Cui Ruhong, and others to the newspaper, where they sealed up all the machinery and public property and then took it over. The newspaper, believing that it was fighting for justice and would not avoid any sacrifice, was unable to resist and was forcibly taken over. The newspaper immediately telegraphed the Central Government to report everything and published advertisements in various newspapers, describing the circumstances of being ordered to cease publication and declaring that if anyone used the newspaper's name for counter-revolutionary propaganda, all circles should not be deceived.

Furthermore, on the 18th, the Peiping Garrison Command sent Li, along with nearly a hundred armed military police, to the North China Daily and the Peiping branch of the Central News Agency, both established in Peiping by the Central Party Headquarters. Claiming to be acting on Yan Xishan's orders, they ordered the paper to cease publication, drove out the staff, and then sealed it up. Around 4 PM, Li claimed to be acting on orders from the Garrison Command and took over all the newspaper's public property. The newspaper, oppressed by violence and unable to resist, could only allow it to be destroyed. The responsible personnel, besides telegraphed the Central Government to report everything and also published advertisements in Peiping and Tianjin newspapers, declaring the circumstances of being forcibly shut down, stating that before resuming publication, it would not be responsible for any illegal actions taken under its name.

Local dispatches

Jiading

A robbery occurred in Chengqiao Town: At the Chen Rice Milling Factory in Chengqiao Town, outside the east gate, around 8 PM last night, suddenly six robbers speaking with a Hakka accent and wearing short clothes, brandishing pistols, ordered no one to make a sound and proceeded to rob the factory. A total of more than twenty silver dollars were stolen. By the time the police squad from the Public Security Bureau in the city received the news and dispatched a team to intercept them, they had already disappeared.

A boat selling water caltrop was robbed at night: At the Lijiaku area of Jiwang Town in the county, a boat selling water caltrop from Zhenjiang was moored on the night of the 22nd, returning to Shanghai after selling its goods. The boat owner, surnamed Wang, was carrying 1,500 yuan in cash, which was discovered by thieves. Around 1 AM that night, they stole everything. The boat owner struggled with the thieves and was shot and killed on the spot, along with a female member of the crew. By the time the town's security corps received the news and arrived, the thieves were already gone.

Kunshan

The county government burned smoking paraphernalia: At 10 AM on the 23rd, the Kunshan County Government publicly burned the opium and smoking paraphernalia confiscated from January 18th to February 19th in front of the auditorium. The High Court specially sent County Magistrate Lin of Taicang to Kunshan to supervise the burning, which was completed at noon.

The Finance Bureau fears reassignment: Wang Huazhao, Director of the Kunshan County Finance Bureau, was reassigned by order of the Finance Department to be the Director of the Qingpu Finance Bureau. His vacancy was filled by Li Fazhen. Director Li arrived in Kunshan on the 22nd and was scheduled to take office on the 24th.

Zhangpu Town was looted by bandits: At noon on the 23rd, more than ten bandit boats, carrying over a hundred lake bandits, fully armed, suddenly arrived in Zhangpu Town, in the seventh district of the county. After landing, they secretly deployed sentries, first cutting the telephone lines, then going to the Public Security Bureau branch and monitoring the police officers, seizing four rifles. Then they went to the security corps and seized twelve rifles. Squad leader Li Daoying was shot by bandits. The bandits left at 4 PM, kidnapping many people.

Suzhou

Actively preparing to build the Fifth Prison: President Lin of the High Court previously ordered President Huang of the Zhenjiang District Court to find and purchase 140 mu of farmland outside the east gate of the county to build the Fifth Jiangsu Prison. He had sent Shi Zechen, Director of the Prison Section, to Zhenjiang to inspect it and reported it in the records. Now, President Lin, regarding whether the land price checked by President Huang of the county was accurate, specially sent personnel again to jointly estimate the land price with the local Land Review Committee, and then allocated funds to purchase the land and recruit workers for construction.

Western detective came to Suzhou to arrest bandits: The Shanghai Public Concession Police Force, based on a report that a major criminal, Gu Sanxin, who had been robbing in the concession, was hiding in Donggangjing area on the border of Suzhou and Changshu. After receiving the report, the police force, on the 23rd, ordered a Western detective to come to Suzhou to meet with Zhao Henglong, a detective from the third district of the Water Police, and hire a motorboat to go to Donggangjing to secretly arrest the criminal. However, Gu had already fled after hearing the news. The Western detective returned to Shanghai yesterday to report back.

Ni Bi and others continued to open an investigation court: Ni Bi, Ge Jianshi, Gu Ziyang, and secretaries Gu Shuyin, Chen Baixin, Ge Shangde, Wang Zhiren, and others, former executive committee members of the Provincial Executive Committee, were detained and sent to the Suzhou High Court for investigation on suspicion of counter-revolutionary activities. After the prosecutor filed a public prosecution, a court investigation was opened on the 4th of this month. Although Ni and others were released on bail, Lin Dawen, the first division chief of the High Court, also scheduled to continue the court investigation this afternoon (the 25th) and summoned Ni and others to the court for questioning.

Sun Bosheng was sued again: Sun Bosheng, a wealthy businessman from Changshu who owned the New Hui Zhong and Old Hui Zhong hotels in Shanghai, was sued last year by Wu Yucheng and his wife, the parents of his concubine Wu Meiying, in the Shanghai court for Sun's rape of their young daughter Meiyun (i.e., Meiying's younger sister). The court clarified that Wu Yucheng's two daughters, Meiying and Meiyun, were both accepted by Sun Bosheng as concubines, and there was no forced rape. The trial concluded that Sun Bosheng was innocent. At that time, relatives and friends of both parties mediated a settlement and signed a settlement agreement. Recently, Wu Yucheng claimed that Sun was unwilling to fulfill the settlement agreement and sued Sun again to the Changshu County Government in his original place. After repeated summonses and inquiries, no judgment has been made. And Wu Yucheng came to Suzhou again the other day and filed a petition with the High Court, stating that because the defendant was rich and powerful and Changshu was within his sphere of influence, the trial member scolded and reprimanded the plaintiff during the trial without explanation. Therefore, he requested a transfer of jurisdiction for the trial to ensure justice, etc. It is still unknown whether the High Court will approve this.

Songjiang

The Dagangjing River has begun surveying for major dredging: The Dagangjing River, within the first district of this city, reaches the Huangpu River to the south, with frequent boat traffic and is related to the prosperity of the market. Recently, due to severe siltation, the county government decided to dredge it in the county government meeting, first ordering the Construction Bureau to survey it and then carry out the construction. The funds required for the survey, according to the budget prepared by the bureau, were over 190 yuan, which was reported to the county government and Zhuang Jiankang, the director of the steamboat convenience association, donated the survey funds last month and submitted them to the county government. Now, the Construction Bureau has dispatched technicians and staff to begin the survey.

Meningitis discovered in the urban area: Meningitis was discovered in Xinzhuang Town of this county last month, and the momentum has subsided slightly in recent days. However, cases have been discovered in the urban area in recent days, and the public is very alarmed.

Qingpu

A large number of refugees arrived at Guanyintang: Yesterday evening, over two hundred boats of refugees from Hunan arrived in Guanyintang Town in the eleventh district of Qingpu from the Xiaokunshan area, numbering about three thousand people. Residents were extremely frightened. Subsequently, the town head rewarded them with five dan of white rice, two dan of vegetables, and some cash, and the refugees started to leave the town and headed towards Chonggu.

Zhang Zhongzhai's grandson was kidnapped by bandits: Zhang Zhongzhai, an old man from Xishengjiadai of Datuanhe Beach near Zhujiajiao Town in Qingpu, was already in his sixties. He worked as an accountant at Wu Haizha's house in Zhujiajiao. His wife had passed away early, and he only had one grandson named Jisheng, who was already twenty years old. Last year, kidnappings were prevalent in that area. Fearing that they would be affected, Zhang had his grandson live elsewhere. Now that the situation had calmed down a bit, the grandson returned home. Unexpectedly, around 9 PM on the 21st, more than ten bandits speaking with a local accent, holding Mauser pistols, broke in through the window, dragged his grandson out of bed, and kidnapped him to a bandit boat. Last night, more than twenty bandits came again, openly armed, negotiating a ransom with Zhang, asking for 10,000 yuan. Zhang was not a wealthy household and could not reach an agreement. It is unknown how it will be resolved.

Fengxian

An accomplice died of illness in prison: Xu Yongchao, an accomplice in the Zhuanghang arson and robbery case, was arrested and sent to the county for interrogation by Team Leaders Ding and Yang of the county police, and then transferred to the Suzhou High Court for trial and sentencing last December. Now, according to Suzhou, the prisoner has died of illness in prison this month, so his family will go to transport the body back for burial within a few days.

Strange news of a ghost possessing someone: Miss Luo, the mistress of Dongfu Garden in Zhuanghang East Market, was suddenly possessed by a ghost around 6 PM last night and fainted. The family sought medical attention in panic. The woman spoke in a male voice, claiming to be her deceased husband, Arong, recounting past events in detail without error, saying that he had gone to burn incense at Xiaopubo and happened to see his son AGen, so he followed him home to visit, without any other intention. It is said that Arong died in a bandit case fifteen years ago, and for the past five years, around Qingming Festival, he has possessed his wife and spoken to people as if he were still alive, which is a very strange thing.

Nantang held a dam opening: The opening date of the Nanqiao Pond Dam was originally scheduled for March 20th, but because the department commissioner had not yet inspected it, and the project had already stopped, the East and West River Bureaus specially prepared reasons for urgently opening the dam and submitted them to the Construction Department for review. On the other hand, today (the 23rd), they issued a notice to all large and small ponds in the entire pond area to open up at once.

Wuxi

The County Magistrate rectifies silk cocoons: During the first county administration meeting this year, the Wuxi County Government proposed to rectify silk cocoons, establish a sericulture school, and organize a roving lecturing sericulture group in seventeen districts. All silk factories should establish female workers' training institutes. The meeting decided (1) to temporarily retain the sericulture school, and discuss the method of inspecting silkworm seeds separately; (2) the county-level sericulture field should jointly guide farmers in sericulture methods with the district offices; (3) all silk factories should establish female workers' training institutes to improve the silk-making skills of workers. County Magistrate Sun believes that this county is a prosperous area for sericulture and silk cocoons, and the production volume is the richest. He should urgently find a way to comply, and yesterday he specially instructed the County Chamber of Commerce to forward a letter to all silk factories to comply.

The head of the Baojia system will be abolished soon: The Wuxi County Government previously received a provincial order to abolish the name of the Baojia head in all counties. Chen Liangdong, Director of the Finance Bureau, believes that the Baojia head is responsible for urging tax payment, and it has never been easy to collect silver taxes in Wuxi. If the Baojia head is abolished, it will definitely have an impact. He specially requested instructions from the Finance Department. Former Director Zhang Shuyong believes that in fact, the Baojia head is indeed still necessary to exist, but since it has been clearly ordered to be abolished, it should be followed. However, the law and the facts must be considered, and it may be possible to abolish the Baojia head in name, and grant a different name to those who can be honest and law-abiding, and supervise them to urge tax payment, and then replace them when the neighborhood chiefs are produced in the future. After Director Chen returned to Wuxi, he has drafted reform measures, and will implement them after the county administration meeting decides.

Follow-up news after the case of shooting and killing two people was solved: Yang Xianyi, who opened Yanzike in Sibao Village outside the North Gate of Xiyi, his son Jinquan and cook Wu Rongsheng, were shot and killed by roving soldiers. Because of his eagerness to avenge, Yang waited day and night. Soon after, he arrested Liu Keli, wearing a uniform, in a certain opium den in Jiucheng Village, believing that he was indeed the main culprit, and sent him to the county government. The county government put him in fetters and detained him. Unexpectedly, around 12:00 that night, a person resembling an official led thirty or forty armed men to meet with County Magistrate Sun and forcibly demanded Liu Keli. The next day, they forcibly demanded the plaintiff Yang Xianyi from County Magistrate Sun, and County Magistrate Sun finally gave up after arguing strongly. Now, County Magistrate Sun has requested instructions from the Songhu Garrison Commander when he went to Shanghai to attend the bandit suppression meeting, and Yang Xianyi is also afraid of other dangers and has taken his whole family to Changshu to avoid disaster.

The reorganization issue of the Civilian Vocational Training Center: The civilian vocational training center in this county previously decided at a board of directors meeting to reorganize into a public relief home. The vice director of the center, Wu, rushed to complete the various affairs in the center, but the county government has not made any statement yet. Recently, Vice Director Wu felt that it was increasingly difficult to maintain the various affairs in the center, and yesterday he sent another letter to County Magistrate Sun, requesting him to send personnel to take over the reorganization quickly.

Water police guarding against lake bandits: Dongting Xishan area has always been a place where lake bandits come and go. District Chief Wang Songbao of that district, because the bandit forces in the lake have been rampant recently, and there have been incidents of intercepting ships and kidnapping people for ransom, specially telegraphed to the second district of the water police to quickly dispatch ships to suppress them. Commander Mao, after receiving the telegram, in addition to ordering the seventh team leader Wang Wusheng to send a team nearby to guard against bandits, specially dispatched two patrol ships again yesterday to cooperate in prevention and consolidate lake defense.

Dingchang Silk Factory's work stoppage resolved: Dingchang Silk Factory on Nanxin Road outside the South Gate of this county issued door passes to restrict the free entry and exit of female workers to avoid accidental losses. All the female workers in the factory expressed their opposition and went on strike at 10:00 AM the day before yesterday, demanding that the factory cancel the door passes. Subsequently, manager Qian Feng of the factory and Gao Kaiqie explained, and representatives from the Silk Factory Workers' Union went to mediate. The female workers finally understood and resumed work as usual yesterday (the 24th).

The rice price in the county has skyrocketed: Recently, due to the scarcity of guest rice arrivals from Anhui and other provinces, and some profiteering merchants privately transporting large quantities of rice out of the county, the rice price has skyrocketed. Yesterday, high-quality white rice had risen to 15 yuan and 8 jiao per stone, and there is a trend of continued increases. The poor and suffering people are all terrified, and deeply hope that the government will quickly find a way to dredge the source, strictly prohibit private transportation, and suppress the rice price to maintain people's food.

Changzhou

Bandits robbed passenger ships in a row: Two passenger ships from Wu Yi Xiaohe set sail to the city on the night of the 22nd. When passing through the Xihegang area of ​​Shuita Township, suddenly three bandits, each holding a pistol, shouted at the boatman on the shore to stop the ship. One thief was standing guard on the shore, and two thieves boarded the ship to rob it. First, the boat of Tang Jinhai, the owner of the passenger boat, was looted, and then the boat of Yan Kunsheng, the owner of the passenger boat, was robbed. Passengers and silver and gold jewelry on the ships were completely robbed.

The Hangzhou Training Regiment will open training in Changzhou: The Central Army Officer Training Regiment stationed in Hangzhou, Zhejiang Province, recently received an order from Commander-in-Chief Chiang to open up and step up training in Changzhou, hoping to become an elite division. The regiment specially sent Li Jianbang, the chief of the General Affairs Barracks Section, to Changzhou on the 23rd to contact the military barracks. He has already surveyed and designated Chongfa Temple, the County Confucian Temple, Qingliang Temple, and Tianning Temple as training barracks. After Chief Li completed the contact, he returned to Hangzhou to report in the afternoon.

Nantong

The Marine Corps stationed in Tonghai suppresses the communists: In various districts of East Road, Nantong, there are large groups of communists, combined with bandits, calling themselves the Red Army, carrying out large-scale harassment. On the night of the 21st, they suddenly surrounded and disarmed the third squadron of the county police team stationed in the Si Jiaba Si Yang Ba area, with great momentum. The pseudo-command headquarters was set up in Touqiao Town, and bandit sentries were densely deployed within seventy or eighty li from east to west. The county government, in view of the emergency situation, immediately requested assistance from the navy anchored outside Lujing Port. Captain Ying Rui and Captain Li of the Hai Chou immediately dispatched the Marine Corps to land, carrying a large number of machine guns and submachine guns. The headquarters was set up in the Clubhouse. On the 23rd, a team patrolled the streets. Another team, led by Staff Officer Liu Huanqian, Deputy Ye Jinqin, and Deputy Li Xianggang, used the Public Security Bureau to guide them and drove to the bandit area in a car to suppress them. County Magistrate Chen also agreed with the Songhu Garrison Headquarters in Shanghai to send a battalion to Tong on the night of the 23rd to suppress the bandits. The provincial government also telegraphed the county government to the effect that it had dispatched the 17th squadron of the provincial police force and would arrive in Tong to cooperate in the suppression as soon as possible. Recently, the East Road telephone and telegraph lines above Erjia Town were cut off by bandits, and the news was not available. The county police team and the chief police team machine gun team are currently concentrated in Erjia Town, Yuxi area. The second squadron of the county police team stationed in Yudong has been cut off by bandits. Wu Xuzhai's detachment, the squadron leader of the first squadron, only escaped with 18 policemen, and Wu's whereabouts are unknown. This time, the county police team suffered heavy losses. All sectors of the local community are extremely dissatisfied with Yan Diannan, the captain of the team. After the Marine Corps set out to suppress the bandits, various ships continued to dispatch more than one hundred soldiers to the city to shuttle through the city and use freight cars to transport a large number of bullets to the front for use. Tonight (the 23rd) is still temporarily under martial law, but the people's hearts have been stabilized.

The issue of raising funds to repair dams: Tiansheng Port and the 14th and 15th Dams west of Tongyi were washed away by the tide, and the river bank is becoming more dangerous. The Construction Bureau is dispatching personnel to estimate and plans to add embankments downstream of the collapsed dam and connect them with the original dam to better resist the tide. The total cost is more than 39,000 yuan. The county government will soon convene people from all walks of life to discuss fundraising methods.

The Nantong-Haimen native cloth industry resumed wheel transport: The large-scale native cloth in Nantong and Haimen counties is sold exclusively to the three northeastern provinces. In the past, the industry was transported north by wheels via the outer sea. Later, the Shabugong Institute transported it, hiring sand boats. Now, each village is concerned that sand boats transporting north have a lot of risk and it is difficult to meet market demand, so they have all resumed wheel transport.

Rugao

Communist bandits from Nantong harassed Juegang: At 6 PM on the 19th, 500 to 600 communists with more than 100 rifles and dozens of submachine guns were discovered in the Shuangdun Town area of Juegang City, which is connected to Nantong County. They suddenly fled north to Yang'an Township in the Juegang District, extorting guns from the security corps and confiscating many self-defense guns from the homes of the local people Zhu Xuemin and Ding Weibao. The houses were also burned down.

Chezhen police and regiment jointly suppressed the bandit: Yesterday, the third branch of the Chemahu Qingxiang Office reported that the bandits Xue Jiu and others were gathering in the Xuejiayao area to burn and kill at will. They dispatched the first squad stationed in Xiaoweiqiao and the first squadron stationed in Che to jointly suppress the bandits with the Guoyuan Security Corps.

Li Tongshan's entire family was brutally killed by bandits: Li Tongshan in the E'dai area of Lugang District was a small well-off family and opened an oil mill. The other day, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came and killed all seven members of Li's family, men, women, old and young, with guns or knives, and none were spared.

Jiangyin

Bandits are rampant in the southeast countryside: Chen Aisheng and two other men from the Wuguan Changpujing in the Sanquan Township were well-off. The other day, they were asked by the bandit leaders Lu Zhanglin and Qin Qirong to borrow 1,300 yuan. Chen Aisheng needed 500 yuan and asked to send it to Xiangshan. Chen Jitang needed 500 yuan and asked to send it to Shizi Bridge. Chen Junfang needed 300 yuan and asked to send it to Dongqingshu within three days. Zhang Xianting's home in Changshou Miaojia Lane was visited by eight or nine bandits the night before last, and borrowed 200 yuan, which they were limited to collect in two days.

Settled cases from the autumn survey in the 18th year of the Republic: The Finance Bureau received an order from the Finance Department to prepare and send a comparative table of the actual collection of silver and rice from the autumn survey in the 18th year of the Republic, and the report was completed yesterday. The original amount in Jiangyi was equivalent to 1,013,620.05 mu of flat land. Except for 29,027.77 mu of old wasteland and public occupation, and 130,301.27 mu of unharvested land due to insect disasters in the 18th year, the amount of matured flat land in the autumn survey was 854,291.11 mu, and the silver to be collected per mu was 1 qian, 5 li, and 6 hao, and the rice to be collected was 5 sheng, 5 he, and 4 shao. According to statistics, the actual collection of upper and lower busy silver under the matured land item was 90,298 yuan, 2 qian, 5 fen, and 8 li, which is equivalent to 185,111.427 yuan of silver dollars at 2.05 yuan per tael. The actual collection of rice was 47,358 shi, 4 sheng, 7 he, and 7 shao, which is equivalent to 236,790.28 yuan of silver dollars at 5 yuan per shi. Recently, due to bad weather, true meningitis was suddenly discovered in the area of ​​Nangwai Langchuanbang, and the infection rate was extremely rapid.

Zhenjiang

Active progress of the National Exhibition: The Jiangsu Provincial National Goods Exhibition was originally scheduled to open on March 15th, but it was postponed due to insufficient preparation. Also, the Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Goods could not come to Zhenjiang immediately due to the relationship between the All-Zhejiang Disaster Relief Association and the National Goods Temporary Commercial Ground. Now, everything is about to be ready. Factories in Shanghai have also publicly elected representatives to come to Zhenjiang on the 26th to handle various matters. Zhang Daofan, a standing committee member of the provincial party department, and He Yushu, director of the Department of Agriculture and Mines, have all agreed to serve as review committee members of the association, and it is expected to open in early April.

Yangzhou

Privately transported wheat ships were released by the county magistrate: The Jiangdu County Restructuring Committee and the Public Security Bureau respectively issued letters ordering Zhou Peizhi, a patrol officer of the Huojiaqiao Public Security Branch Bureau, to investigate and seize 72 privately transported wheat ships, totaling 26,061 packages and weighing more than 30,000 stones. Now, Tao Zhonghe, the director of the Restructuring Committee, because the county magistrate recognized that the wheat was transported to Shanghai and not exported overseas, should be released immediately. Tao personally went to investigate the situation, and the ship was indeed parked in the Han River, with a tendency to wait for a river steamer to transfer the goods. When asked about the承之aspects, he only said that it was transported to Shanghai. However, he could not point out the company name or factory number, which is of great research value.

The case of the Baolun Temple monk has been withdrawn: The case of monk Fayu and others accusing monk Xianzong of Baolun Temple was accepted by the county for many years, and all walks of life were very interested. Now, the plaintiff has submitted a request to the county to withdraw the case, and it has been approved, stating that the report is known. The investigation of this case has been going on for a long time, but no factual evidence has been found. Now that all the temple properties have been clearly investigated by the Buddhist Association monks, the prosecution will not be initiated in accordance with Article 244, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law.

Funing

The Provincial Department ordered the cessation of the two-corner surtax: Zhou Qiu, Director of the Funing County Finance Bureau, believed that the two-corner surtax under the land tax miscellaneous funds in this county in the 18th year of the Republic was to offset the shortage of Cao rice in Liu County. He had previously reported it to the Finance Department, but it has now been rejected. However, because it concerns the local needs, he specially invited various agencies to the county government for a meeting at 2:00 PM today (the 18th) to discuss it together. After public discussion, it was decided that since the order to reject it had been issued, it should be stopped immediately.

Disaster relief personnel dispatched to distribute relief: The county disaster relief association believes that tens of thousands of starving people in Chenjiayang Wufanggang and other places are waiting to be fed, so today (the 19th) it dispatched personnel to carry funds to distribute relief.

The giant bandit Wang Xiangfan resisted arrest and was killed: At the second watch last night, a dozen bandits suddenly came to the Yutou Town Public Security Branch Station in the southern countryside of this county, wanting to rob the station of guns. The scout police learned about it, and the patrol officer Guo Baoguo ordered the patrol police to lie in ambush in the ditch. Before long, the bandits came to the station, the police called out, and the bandits opened fire, and the soldiers also returned fire. The two sides fought for half an hour, and one bandit was killed on the spot. The body was identified by the public as the famous giant bandit Wang Xiangfan. A pistol and two bullets were found next to the bandit's body. He was the main criminal in the case of the shooting and killing of Wang Baoxiang, the adjutant of the Ninth Army, last year, and he had not been arrested despite repeated arrests. Today (the 21st), the County Public Security Bureau has reported the situation to the county government.

Jiashan

The robbery case in Luxu was found to be a false rumor: At 3:00 PM on the 22nd, there was another rumor of a robbery case in Luxu. After a detailed investigation, it was a false rumor, and the local area was as peaceful as ever.

The rice price has risen repeatedly, and people's food is worrying: The current market rice price is soaring, and it is rising every day. Buyers from all over are gathering, and the current price for ordinary grain is 14 yuan and 7 jiao per dan, and the winter double sale price is 15 yuan and 7 jiao. The trend is still rising. The current party and government authorities are urgently seeking to suppress the rice price to maintain people's livelihood.

A rice boat was robbed while passing through Di Zao: Yesterday, a rice boat belonging to Huang A'ao from Huzhou was robbed by bandits at the port of Xitang Di Zao, losing 87 stones of rice, 64 yuan of silver, and many sundries.

Inspection of stamps creates a trend: Zhu Hua and Zhu Wu Xingzhu, inspectors of the Pingjia stamp tax bureau, went to Wang Rixin's rice store outside the West Gate to inspect the stamps. Because they did not bring police, they had a conflict with Wang Rixin, the store owner, and were arrested by each other and taken to the Public Security Bureau. According to Wang Rixin, he lost 300 yuan. The stamp bureau claimed that Wang had privately arrested public officials and sent a letter requesting investigation and prosecution. It is now heard that both parties have filed lawsuits with the County Court.

Hangzhou

The county magistrate examination is scheduled: The chief and assistant examiners for the third Zhejiang County Magistrate Examination have been appointed. According to news from the Department of Civil Affairs, Minister Zhu Jiahua has contacted the chief and assistant examiners during his trip to Beijing, and the examination will be held on April 10th.

The Hangzhou-Pingyao Highway is open to traffic: The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau issued a letter to all sectors in the name of Zhang Renjie yesterday, stating that the opening ceremony of the Hangzhou-Pingyao Highway in this province will be held at 9:00 AM on March 30th.

Germans investigate tea production: Mr. Xiao Sugen (transliteration) from the Economic Committee of Berlin, Germany, came to Zhejiang to investigate tea roasting methods, storage methods, tea land geology, fertilizer application, and recent tea production. The provincial government received a letter from the Bureau of Industry and Commerce yesterday, requesting it to instruct the competent authorities to guide and protect them.

Letter to the Editor

Memorial Week at the Central Government and National Government

▲ Central Party Headquarters: At 9:00 AM on the 24th, the Central Party Headquarters held the 52nd weekly memorial service for the late Premier Sun Yat-sen in the Grand Auditorium. Central Committee members Sun Ke, Shao Yuanchong, Chen Lifu, Chen Yao, and others, as well as officials from various departments and guests, totaling about 500 people, attended. Chairman Sun Ke presided over the ceremony, after which Shao Yuanchong delivered a political report, broadly stating that recently reactionary forces have colluded and exploited each other, attempting to resist the Central Government. All comrades recognize that this is significantly related to the security of the Party and the nation and that work should be intensified to cope with it. However, this is a temporary problem, and it is necessary to quickly resolve it with the power of the Party. At the same time, more attention must be paid to the fundamental problems of the country, that is, the problem of people's livelihood, which the Premier's Founding Program and the Three Principles of the People emphasize first. There must be a good solution to stabilize the lives of the general public. To stabilize the lives of the people, it is necessary to work hard on economic construction and not stop or abandon its basic work due to temporary changes, which would hinder the implementation of political tutelage. The most important basic works during the period of political tutelage are economic construction, local autonomy, education of the Three Principles of the People, and mass training, frugality campaigns, etc. No matter how the environment changes and how difficult it is, if we can continue to work hard with a consistent spirit, then even if reactionary facts continue to occur, the foundation of the Party will never be shaken. In the scope of economic construction, agriculture, industry, and transportation must all have considerable development, but it is especially important to recognize agriculture as the mother of industry and commerce, and strive to improve it to increase production, so that the economy can avoid lagging behind. The American industrial sector is less complex than the British one, and disputes do not occur because American agriculture is developed and can accommodate a large number of workers, allowing them to live a stable life. Because the industrial sector has a considerable solution to its own livelihood, it is unwilling to change. China has been established on agriculture since ancient times. According to the current social situation, the starting point for political and economic construction must be the development of agriculture, so that the productive capacity of each person can maintain the life of one person, and the natural production can be developed and circulated as much as possible, so as to conform to the ancient training of adapting to and using resources for the benefit of the people, and gradually achieve the goal of the principle of people's livelihood. As for the two words "respect virtue," absolute attention should also be paid, so that the society and the public can cultivate their morality, seek benefits for the public, and make knowledge and culture progress day by day, so as to lead the improvement of economic undertakings and satisfy the desires of the people's lives. In this way, the disadvantages of treating the head when it hurts and treating the foot when it hurts can be avoided. The purpose of the Principle of People's Livelihood is to nourish the people, which is different from the purpose of capitalism to make profits. It must be good at using it so that capitalism does not become imperialism, and the Principle of People's Livelihood does not become capitalism. For thousands of years, China has been governed and disordered alternately. The main reasons are all due to the influence of the problem of people's livelihood, which leads to changes. Now the people suffer from famine, war, and harsh taxes, which make them unable to live. It is all too common to see this. Most of the spirit should be used to solve this fundamental problem, so that the people can recuperate, which is the true ability and performance of party members to serve the country, society, and people. I hope all comrades will work hard, and so on. The meeting adjourned after the report.

▲ National Government: At 10:00 AM on the same morning, the National Government held a weekly memorial service for the late Premier Sun Yat-sen. Tan Yankai, Gu Yingfen, He Yingqin, Chen Yi, Zhou Yawei, Liu Ruiheng, Jiang Menglin, Li Jinlun, Zhang Wohua, and others, as well as all the staff of the Civil Affairs Office and the Military Affairs Office, totaling more than 200 people, attended. Chairman Tan Yankai presided over the ceremony. After the ceremony, Secretary Qian Changzhao delivered a political report as follows: [There is a widespread movement in the Far East, which is worth paying attention to, that is, the national self-determination movement. Last October in India, the Governor-General of India issued a speech on Indian autonomy, and the gradually spreading independence movement was slightly broken, but after the National Congress, the situation became tense again. Recently, the relationship between Britain and India has deteriorated, and non-violent resistance has already begun. It is difficult to predict the outcome. In Korea last November, the Gwangju student riots were tense. Japan established an autonomous educational system through the Governor-General of Korea to create a harmonious atmosphere. In January of this year, workers joined the resistance, and the general Korean people were extremely激昂. The independence movement will continue. The Philippine independence issue has become increasingly heated since this year. Last month, the Independence Congress issued a declaration listing fourteen reasons, separately explaining that the United States must immediately allow the Philippines to be completely independent. It is not easy for the United States to deal with this time. It is still unknown whether it can be recovered. In Vietnam this year, the revolutionary voice is quite high. According to news from Paris, many revolutionaries have been sentenced to death. The high-pressure means of France may not be able to solve it thoroughly. We know that Britain and India, Japan and Korea, the United States and the Philippines, and France and Vietnam all have major political and economic relations. A change will not only cause local problems, but also cause problems in the Far East. Not only will problems occur in the Far East, but also in the whole world. Brothers personally speculate that the independence movements in India, Korea, the Philippines, and Vietnam have arisen, although they have occurred at different times, and if they succeed, they will succeed at the same time, because as long as one place succeeds, the others will definitely be like a storm, and they cannot be cleaned up. The Pacific War may occur because of this. It is important to know that some of the so-called independence movements are completely automatic, some are automatic and need the secret assistance of another country's power, and some are completely passive and controlled by another country. Complete automation is a very good expression of national spirit. Automation and the need for assistance from other countries are quite dangerous. As for being completely passive and controlled by another country, it is like driving away the tiger from the front door and letting the wolf in from the back door, which is extremely dangerous. We hope that the national self-determination in the Far East is completely automatic, but now the countries chasing deer in the Pacific are suspicious of each other and guard against each other. None of Britain, Japan, the United States, and France are willing to relax a little, and their important colonies are demanding independence, regardless of whether there is a third party instigating them, they always think that other countries are making trouble there. Since the interests are significant, it is possible to take this opportunity to cause a war. If the Pacific does not have a war, it is over. If a war occurs, our country will be in the middle of it and will have to make sacrifices. Therefore, today, when we talk about the national self-determination movement in the Far East, we should also arouse the attention of our compatriots. Recently, Feng and Yan have cooperated, and at the same time, they have used all means to contact all kinds of reactionaries to make trouble. This rebellion is very large in scope. For them, it is the last struggle, and for the Central Government, it is also the key to the success of the revolution. After this rebellion, the people of the whole country can understand that the Central Government's aim is peace. Until it is absolutely necessary, we will not use force. After this, we can let everyone know that the most recent object of the revolution is the feudal warlords. After this rebellion, the revolutionary comrades can be more united. After this rebellion, the foundation of the Party and the country can be absolutely consolidated, and there will be no more rebellions in the future. As for the Central Government's attitude towards this rebellion, Chairman Chiang has made a solemn statement at the memorial week last Monday, that is, to be steady and persevering, to control the situation with inaction, and to clean up the overall situation with great certainty. What is worrying is that the people of the whole country are affected by the rebellion and still cannot live and work in peace. They indirectly sacrifice for the revolution. After the government puts down the rebellion, the only most important task is to reduce the burden and suffering of the people. This is not just empty talk. In fact, if the people are not appeased, the vitality of the society will never be restored, and the revolution will never succeed. Everyone who hears about the death of Mr. Liang Zhongjia mourns for him. Last time, when the Russian army invaded the border, Mr. Liang took the lead and risked his life to defend the country and protect the people. In the midst of great difficulties, he still wrote to his friends, saying that whoever dares to lose an inch of land will not see his countrymen. His sacrifice to foreign countries can be a model for soldiers. Now that the Sino-Russian negotiations have come to an end, Mr. Liang has suddenly passed away. It is probably due to the mental stimulation and physical pain of the past year that led to this. Mr. Liang has been in office for more than ten years and has not acquired any property. After his death, he was desolate, and his grandmother and father had no one to support them, and his children were still underage. The government should give him preferential treatment and condolences. However, the death of Mr. Liang has become a major loss to our country. I only hope that the compatriots of the whole country will work hard to strengthen themselves so that the imperialists can no longer trample on us. Then, Mr. Liang can be comforted in the afterlife.]

Sun Dianying's Troops Withdraw from Guide

A communication from Xuzhou on the 22nd stated that Sun Dianying's troops had suddenly moved. Han Fuju requested the Central Government to thoroughly resolve the issue and telegraphed Liu Zhi, requesting him to send troops to assist in the suppression to achieve the effect of a pincer attack.

As for the Sun's troops on the western route, they had already surrendered their weapons ahead of schedule. Gu, under pressure, sent his representative, Chen Tao, from Guide to Xuzhou on the evening of the 20th to personally visit Liu Zhi and ask him to intercede with the Central Government, expressing his willingness to comply with the order to gather his troops on the north bank of the Yellow River.

However, he requested a delay and asked him to forward a telegram to Han Fuju, asking him not to attack again. Liu agreed to forward the message on his behalf. Chen returned to Guide at noon on the 21st to report. However, on that day, clashes occurred between Sun's troops and Han's troops between Lanfeng and Shangqiu, and they refused to move their defense.

The two sides fought fiercely for half a day. Sun's troops were defeated and hurriedly withdrew from Guide that night, retreating towards Tuocheng, Taikang, Luyi, and Zhoukou, intending to cross the Pinghan Line and retreat towards Fangcheng and Nanyang in western Henan.

It was learned that there was no trace of Sun's troops in Guide.

This morning, Liu Zhi sent Liang Huasheng's division of four regiments and the Great Wall armored train from Xuzhou West to Dangshan and Muma 集.

In pursuit, the Longhai Railway Bureau also dispatched an engineer today to carry materials and opened a special train to Liu Diquan to rush to repair the railway. It is expected to be completed within a few days, and the transportation between Xuzhou and Bian will be restored. (Zhonghua News Agency)

Arrested Provincial Committee Members in Fujian Completely Sent to the Provincial Capital

A communication from Fuzhou stated that the arrested provincial government members, Cheng Shijun, Xu Xianshi, and Wu Shu, the director of the Maritime Public Security Bureau, were escorted from Yanping to the provincial capital on March 10 and resided in the old ordnance factory in Huangdian. After that, the three provincial government members detained in Youxi, Chen Naiyuan, Zheng Baojing, and Lin Zhiyuan, were also sent to the provincial capital by Wan'an steamship on the 17th and also resided in the ordnance factory in Huangdian. According to the original plan, the six arrested people have been completely sent to the provincial capital and should be sent to Nanjing by Chen Jiliang to ask the Central Government to handle them. Then, the National Government will issue an order to reorganize the provincial government. It is now heard that Lu Xingbang intends to move the six people from the old ordnance factory in Huangdian to the western-style building of the Youth Association summer camp in nearby Hongshan, so that their daily lives can be more comfortable and their families can be allowed to visit them to dispel rumors. After the provincial government is reorganized, they will be sent to Nanjing again. On the 18th, Chen Jiliang and Lu's advisor, Yang Yugu, and Zhang Qun's representative, Guo Shihui, consulted on the Chutong warship in Taijiang. Chen intended to temporarily move the six people to the Chutong warship or the Majiang Naval Social Center, protected by the Navy, to observe the situation and then send them to Nanjing for handling. Yang Yugu telegraphed Lu Xingbang for instructions. Once the reply is received, a decision can be made. As for Liu Heding's 56th Division, which was ordered by the General Headquarters to advance from Quanzhou to the provincial capital, the vanguard of Gui Zhenyuan's brigade has arrived in Fuqing County, near the province, from Putian. Liu Shangzhi's brigade has also arrived in Yongtai from Xianyou, and the governments of the two counties have been ordered to prepare for the application of porters. Chen Jiliang telegraphed Liu Heding yesterday, reporting that the five provincial committee members had all arrived in the province, and the provincial situation had been completely resolved. The defense of the provincial capital has two regiments of the Marine Corps, Huang Maohe and Lin Bingzhou, which are sufficient to maintain it. Please keep your troops stationed in Xingquan to secure the downstream security. It is still unknown whether Liu's troops will stop advancing. (March 19)

Liu Heding Marches into Putian

▲ His Troops, Liu's Brigade, Have Reached Yongtai and Fuqing

A communication from Xiamen stated that after the 56th Division concentrated in Quanzhou, the 167th Brigade, Liu Shangzhi's troops, marched to Putian, and the 168th Brigade, Gui Zhenyuan's troops, marched to Huian. It was originally planned to advance separately to Yongtai, Fuqing, Datian, and Youxi. Later, they received an order from the provincial government to stop advancing at the original locations, because at that time Lu Xingbang was agreeing to send the five provincial committee members back to the province to await the Central Government's decision. Liu's troops immediately complied with the order to stop advancing at the above-mentioned locations, but they still made mobilization preparations in Quanzhou, Huian, and Putian. On the 16th of this month, Liu Heding, the division commander, ordered the special service battalion, artillery battalion, cavalry battalion, and signal squadron to set off completely from Luoyang and enter Huian. At 5:00 PM, he bid farewell to all circles in Quanzhou, stating during the banquet that he would go to the front to supervise his troops. On the morning of the 17th, Liu led the entire division headquarters and guards to set off for Huian. According to news from the division headquarters, Liu's first step was to station in Putian to command. The division headquarters also stationed in Putian. Liu Shangzhi's brigade, which had originally arrived in Putian, also set off on the 16th and advanced towards Yongtai and Fuqing. Gui Zhenyuan's brigade simultaneously advanced from Huian towards Putian. It was heard that after arriving in Putian, they would advance towards Datian and Youxi. The 332nd regiment of Chen Wantai's 166th Brigade, which was stationed in Quanzhou, was originally sent to the outside of the South Gate on the 13th to join the Jinjiang County magistrate to eradicate the tobacco seedlings. It was also transferred back on the 16th and concentrated in Luoyang. It will continue to open Huian and Putian, leaving only Chen Wantai to lead the 331st regiment to guard Quanzhou. Liu's advance this time was extremely rapid. According to the latest telegram from Quanzhou, the vanguard of Liu's brigade has arrived in Yongtai and Fuqing and is advancing towards the provincial capital. As for the five provincial committee members, Xu Xianshi, Cheng Shijun, Lin Zhiyuan, Chen Naiyuan, Zheng Baojing, and Wu Shu, the director of the Maritime Public Security Bureau, they arrived in the province on the 10th and 17th respectively. Chen Jiliang heard that the vanguard of Liu's division had arrived in Yongtai and Fuqing and telegraphed Liu Heding on the 19th, asking him to stop advancing temporarily and not to enter the province rashly. However, whether Liu's division will temporarily station in Putian or still enter the province depends on how the provincial situation develops. (March 21)

Shandong Provincial Government's Plan to Maintain Coastal Security

▲ Will Purchase Four Gunboats and Recruit More Maritime Police

▲ Send Chen Luanshu and Others to Cooperate with Ge and Shen on Solutions

A communication from Qingdao stated that the Shandong Provincial Government, because the coastline of this province extends to more than 2,000 miles, all matters such as maritime security and fishery protection have been lacking. In recent years, piracy has been rampant, and Japanese people often cross the border to fish. Without appropriate measures, maritime security will not be maintained. Recently, Chen Luanshu and Zhu Xi, two provincial committee members, were specially sent to Qingdao to discuss cooperation solutions with Qingdao Mayor Ge Jing'en and Navy Commander Shen Honglie. The result was very satisfactory. Chen and Zhu have already returned to Ji'nan last night. It is heard that the provincial government intends to use 1.5 million yuan for maritime security in the 19th year, first purchasing four gunboats, establishing a maritime public security bureau, and recruiting more maritime police, which is currently in progress.

Northeast Navy Commander Shen Honglie recently came to Qingdao on the Zhaowei warship and thoroughly discussed the joint defense methods of the Navy and Army with Mayor Ge Jing'en. He then took the original ship to Laoshan Bay on the 16th to inspect the ships belonging to the First Fleet. It is heard that Shen believes that the situation is tense and maritime defense is particularly important. He specially convened the captains of each ship at the office of the First Fleet in Laoshan Bay at 2:00 PM today to hold a maritime defense meeting. The heads of the Marine Corps battalion stationed in Qingdao were also ordered to participate in advance. It is heard that the matters discussed were divided into two items: (1) Measures to maintain coastal security; (2) Eliminate pirates within a time limit to consolidate maritime defense. (20th)

Tragic Fire at a Cinema in Jilin

▲ Seventy or Eighty Male and Female Bodies Have Been Recovered

▲ More Than One Hundred People Were Injured and Countless Are Missing

A communication from Shenyang stated that the provincial government received a telegram from Jilin, stating that at 8:00 PM on the 18th, when the Jiyong Cinema in Dadongmen, Jilin Province, was showing a film, a fire suddenly broke out from the film and spread throughout the entire cinema. The entire audience was in chaos, and men, women, old, and young cried out for help. Because the projector was located right at the gate and the cinema did not have an emergency exit, the audience had no way to escape. The police team of the Public Security Bureau received the news and rushed to the rescue, but because the fire was caused by electricity, it was not easy to extinguish. In an instant, the entire cinema was burned to ashes. On the 19th, seventy or eighty male and female bodies were recovered from the ashes. It was heard that there were 152 people burned at the time, and countless people were missing. Most of the dead were upstairs audiences, including Lu, the director of the Jilin Public Security Bureau, and the entire family of a section chief of the Military Law Department of the Deputy Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast Border Defense Army, and Rong's second wife of the Finance Department of the Jilin Provincial Government. It was found that the cinema had only been open for three months, and its entire building was a simple plank wall, so it was easy to catch fire. (20th)

Important News 2

Qingdao Municipal Government Implements Streamlining

▲ Consolidating Nine Bureaus into Five

Since Qingdao was officially designated as a special municipality by the National Government, the former acting mayor, Wu Siyu, established nine bureaus in accordance with the organizational law of special municipalities: Finance, Land, Education, Public Works, Public Utilities, Port Affairs, Public Security, Social Affairs, and Health. In addition, the Qingdao Observatory is affiliated with the municipal government. It is found that the municipal funding of Qingdao, in addition to the customs cooperative loan (about 600,000 yuan per year), has an annual income of about 3 million yuan from pier donations, land taxes, and miscellaneous items. Before the reorganization, the annual expenditure was about 3 million yuan, and the income and expenditure could be offset. After the reorganization into a special municipality, the scale expanded, and the expenditure increased sharply. Administrative expenses have always been insufficient, and various construction projects have been unable to proceed. Later, Wu left and Ma (Fuxiang) came, following the old system, and the funding became more and more difficult. They had to find ways to increase revenue (such as collecting banquet donations and entertainment donations) to supplement it. Now Ma has been transferred to the chairman of Anhui Province, and Ge Jing'en has succeeded as mayor. At the beginning of Ge's inauguration, he took the streamlining policy as the guiding principle for governing Qingdao. In recent days, he has made great efforts to consolidate the bureaus. It is heard that the consolidation methods of the bureaus are that the organization of the Port Affairs and Public Security Bureaus has not changed much, the Land Bureau has been merged into the Finance Bureau, the Public Utilities Bureau has been merged into the Public Works Bureau, and the Education Bureau and the Health Bureau have been merged into the Social Affairs Bureau. The Public Works Bureau still has four sections: the first section is the General Affairs Section, the second section is in charge of design, the third section is in charge of public utilities, and the fourth section is in charge of road repair and construction. As for water affairs, it has been separated and renamed the Qingdao Special Municipality Waterworks. Since the Social Affairs Bureau has been merged into the Education and Health Bureaus, the affairs are more complicated than before. In addition to the original sections of the bureau, two more sections, Education and Health, have been added. It is heard that after this streamlining, tens of thousands of yuan can be saved each year, and the saved funds will be transferred to construction. It has been decided to officially implement it from April 1.

Letter from Jinshan County Government

To Whom It May Concern, on the morning of the 21st of this month, a large gang of bandits disturbed Zhujing. The police team of our county and the police of the Public Security Bureau, together with the water police, went forward and attacked fiercely. After five hours, the bandits were defeated. In this battle, the police team soldiers and the Public Security Bureau police officers did not suffer any loss. Today, I read the news column of the 22nd of your newspaper, "The gang of bandits attempted to disturb Zhujing and have been dispersed," which stated that three soldiers of the Jinshan County Public Security Team encountered dozens of defeated bandits in Huangqiao and were robbed of their firearms. This is not consistent with the facts. Please correct it as soon as possible. Jinshan County Government, Jiangsu 3.24

Education and Sports News

Athletes Passing Through Shanghai

The weather has been sunny recently. The National Games will be held in Hangzhou in this bright spring, which is a grand event. The athletes from various provinces and cities who should participate in the conference will come to Shanghai and transfer to Hangzhou in the next few days. Several groups of athletes who have arrived in Shanghai in the past few days have been investigated as follows:

(1) Beijing Athletes

The Beijing Special Municipality athletes attending the National Games departed from Beijing for Tianjin on the 19th by express train at 8:10 PM. They sailed south on the Shinming Steamer on the 20th, arriving in Shanghai at around 5:00 PM on the afternoon of the 23rd. They stayed at the Hongkou Great Hotel on North Sichuan Road. After a one-day layover, they left from the North Station by special express train at 6:00 PM yesterday (the 24th) for Hangzhou. The group comprised a total of 54 male and female athletes, led by Mr. Wang Yaodong, Mr. Teng Shugu (a reporter from the Beijing Daily), Mr. Song Binglin, and Ms. Zhong Zhensun, Ms. Jian Huafen, and Ms. San Jingzhi. The list of athletes is recorded below:

Male Athletes

(1) Track and Field

(2) Athletes' Money Storage

The Games Preparatory Committee, in order to facilitate the temporary storage of money for athletes participating in the Games, the General Affairs Section has planned and is actively preparing to establish an Athletes' Money Storage. It is understood that the purpose of this office is to facilitate safekeeping, and since the duration is temporary, no interest will be paid on the stored money. As for the storage amount, it will be in units of five silver dollars, and odd amounts will not be accepted. The procedures for depositing and withdrawing funds will be based on the issued receipts and the athlete's credentials. A currency exchange will also be set up to exchange silver dollars at market prices.

(3) Games Handbook to be Published Tomorrow

The Games Handbook compiled by the Games Committee has been printed and is now being bound. It is expected to be published and distributed around the 26th of this month. The book contains rich content, with impressive pictures and text.

News

Measures for Refund of Fees for the Closure of Jianda University

▲The Municipal Education Bureau Convenes a Meeting of the Board of Directors to Issue Orders

Private Jianda University is Ordered to Close. The Municipal Education Bureau specifically sent a letter to the eighteen board members of the school on the 22nd to convene a meeting at the Education Bureau on the 21st to discuss measures. A method for refunding fees was decided upon. Yesterday, the Municipal Education Bureau instructed the school's board members Chen Tingfan, Huang Wenshan, and Huang Youfeng, stating, "In order to comply with the order to close Private Jianda University, the various fees paid by students should be promptly refunded. This bureau convened a meeting of the board members on February 22 to discuss the closure measures, and the two resolutions are copied and issued to you. The board members should immediately investigate the exact amount of fees paid by the students and the fees to be refunded and report them to the bureau so that the bank deposit can be appropriately withdrawn and distributed by the school. The students are eagerly awaiting the funds and should not be delayed. This is of utmost importance." Enclosed are two copies of the resolutions: (1) Resolution on the method of refunding student fees: (A) Mr. Huang Wenshan, Mr. Chen Tingfan, and Mr. Huang Youfeng will investigate the exact amount of fees paid by the students. (B) Withdraw a suitable amount from the deposit in the Agricultural and Industrial Bank to refund the various fees owed to the students. (C) If the bank deposit is insufficient, the actual amount will be issued first. (D) Students requesting a refund of fees must register with the school with their payment receipts before April 1; after that date, the request will be invalid. (2) Resolution on repaying debts to other schools: It was resolved that the old Jianda board of directors would sell Jianda's assets to repay the debts in full.

Resignation of the Director of the Municipal Education Bureau from the Presidency of the Self-Government Association

The Shanghai Local Self-Government Research Association intended to invite Special Municipality Mayor Zhang Qun to be the President and Director of the Education Bureau Chen Dezheng to be the Vice President. Mayor Zhang has already declined by letter. Recently, Director Chen also declined by letter, saying, "I am grateful for your trust in entrusting me with the position of Vice President. I should have accepted your command, but I also hold the position of Party Education Officer and do not have time to divide my attention. Therefore, I am unable to take on the responsibilities entrusted to me. I hope for your understanding. I am sending this letter to inform you."

Record of the Bureau Affairs Meeting of the County Education Bureau

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 144th weekly memorial service and bureau affairs meeting yesterday. Those present were Inspector Zhu, Zheng Guozhai, Sun Tingfang, Yao Juechen, Pan Xingsan, Cai Xingsan, Yao Xingshu, Wu Renda, and Ni Boying. Inspector Zhu presided over the meeting, and Ni Boying recorded the minutes. After the usual formalities, the meeting proceeded to report on matters and then discussed the following: (1) How should this year's literacy campaign be planned and implemented? It was resolved to submit the matter for discussion at the second Social Education Agency meeting. (2) Should the request of the Tenth People's School to add a grade be approved? It was resolved that since the school had more than one hundred students (an investigation showed that eighty-six students were actually present), the request to add a grade should be approved for the time being. However, if the number of students decreases, the grade should be merged immediately. (3) Should the Farmers' Education Center originally established at the Third People's School be moved to Shangbin? It was resolved that the Farmers' Education Center attached to the supplementary school, originally at the Third People's School, should be moved to Shangbin Elementary School. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Popular Lecture by the Municipal Education Bureau

The Popular Lecture Group of the Municipal Education Bureau held a popular lecture at the Feihong Municipal Elementary School in Zhabei on March 22. About 600 citizens and students attended. The meeting started at 2:00 PM with the usual formalities. The head of the group, Li Dachao, reported, stating that few citizens in the city were literate, and many were illiterate. Only a handful understood current affairs and had common knowledge. The bureau was holding popular lectures as part of social education. The main purpose was to instill common knowledge and report on recent and easily understood news about the Party and the country. Lectures would be held once a week, and citizens were encouraged to participate actively. Shao Minghe and Shen Junda then gave lectures. After the lectures, the various schools began their performances. The First Elementary School performed [The March 18th Massacre], vividly depicting the tragic scene on March 18, 1926, when various Beijing organizations held a national conference at Tiananmen, went to the State Council to petition, and were surrounded and massacred by the government guards, causing many deaths and injuries. The audience was heartbroken. Jiancheng Elementary School performed two acts, one entitled [Regret It Too Late], which used a contract of sale to illustrate the harm of illiteracy, as a piece of paper was mistakenly written with the contract price, resulting in losses, inspiring people to study. The other was [The Joy of Deep Spring (Dance)], which was exquisite and lively and worth seeing. Feihong performed [Elimination], encouraging people to persevere and strive despite difficulties and obstacles, with profound implications.

Record of the Spring Banquet of the Soochow University Alumni Association in Shanghai

Every year, more than two hundred alumni of Soochow University in Hangzhou gather several times to strengthen their connections. Yesterday (the 23rd) at 7:00 PM was the date of the association's spring banquet, which was held at the Zhongyoutian Restaurant. Dozens of people attended, including Chen Dezheng, Wu Wenwei, Zhang Tinggui, Zhang Tianpei, Jin Haoqing, and Zhang Qingsun. At the banquet, President Wu Wenwei first reported that (1) since Zhu Jingnong and Li Peien became the presidents of the alma mater, the school affairs have been flourishing, and April 19th this year will be the completion ceremony of the new dining hall; (2) the alumni association's 100,000 yuan library movement will begin fundraising, and Chen Dezheng has been appointed as the head of the fundraising team; (3) as a result of the election of new staff members, President Wu Wenwei and Secretary Zhang Qingsun were re-elected, Vice President Chen Dezheng, and Treasurer Zhang Tinggui were re-elected, and Hong Ruixiang was elected as the audit committee member. There was no discussion on the resolution to elect President Zhu as the Deputy Minister of Education. The gathering ended happily around 9:00 PM.
