Falls Asleep After Eating and Falls into the River and Dies

Wang Guiyou, a wharf coolie from Qingkou, 19 years old, was working at the Zhaofeng Road wharf yesterday afternoon. He ate a bowl of noodles for lunch and fell asleep from exhaustion. He accidentally fell into the river. By the time the neighboring coolies heard the news and came to rescue him, it was too late. About an hour later, his body floated to the surface. The police car sent it to the coroner's office for examination.

Male Corpse Found Dead on Steps

At about 6:00 PM yesterday, a man about 40 years old suddenly collapsed on the cement steps at the corner of Yunnan Road, Sixth Ma Road. He was wearing a coarse cloth garment and looked like a villager. The police officer on duty found him and reported it to the police station, which sent detective Zhao Ziren to investigate. The deceased's face was yellow, and it was not known why he died. The body was immediately sent to the coroner's office on Philen Road, scheduled for examination this morning.

Unidentified Male Corpse in the Cemetery

An unidentified male corpse was found in the Jinjiaqiao Bangxi Cemetery in Pudong yesterday morning. He was about 50 years old, wearing a Zhigong woolen robe and a small hat. His appearance suggested that he had been murdered. The bailiff Tang Qingzhou found him and reported it to the local court for examination. The court ordered the body to be taken to the court pending examination.

Woman Smuggles Firearms

At about 11:00 PM the other night, Wang Shuxiu, an inspector of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's water patrol team, led police officers Cui Zhongshan, Zhang Jian, and Nie Mengqin on patrol along the river. When passing the Pudong surface of the Dada Wharf, they saw the Daji Steamboat berthed on the riverside and about to raise anchor. They immediately boarded the ship for inspection and found two Jiangbei women, Wu Zhang and Liu Li, in the cabin. Seeing the police team arrive, they immediately looked flustered. Because their behavior was highly suspicious, they immediately searched the two women and found three shell guns, one Browning pistol, and 350 bullets beside them. They took the witnesses back to the station. Director Xu proposed a preliminary hearing. The two women's testimonies were very cunning and they tried to evade responsibility. Since the case involved carrying firearms, which violated the prohibition, they were ordered to prepare a document together with the guns and bullets and submit it to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation and punishment.

The Requisition of the Meeting of the Wusong River by the Requisition Committee Has Been Rescheduled

▲April 11th

The Construction Committee, previously scheduled to meet on the 25th of this month to discuss the dredging of the Wusong River, and sent letters to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, the Shanghai Special Municipal Government, and the Commercial and Complete Society to send representatives to attend. It is now learned that the Jiangsu Provincial Government is being reorganized and could not send representatives to attend as scheduled. The meeting has been rescheduled to 2:00 PM on April 11th and will still be held at the committee. It is learned that the Shanghai Special Municipal Government has appointed Sun Tuxian, a technician of the Port Affairs Bureau, to attend the meeting at that time.

Shanghai County Political Conference Notes

▲Scheduled Defense Conference

The Shanghai County Government held its 35th county political conference in the county government auditorium yesterday. The conference was chaired by County Chief Leng, with more than ten people in attendance, including the director of the Construction Public Security Bureau. The meeting began as scheduled at 2:00 PM in the afternoon. First, the chairman reported: (1) Regarding the county's public security funding, he had discussed it with Director Shen Jin Province, and the provincial department has submitted it to the provincial government meeting for discussion and decided to raise funds. If there are any difficulties in the future, he will go to the province for further negotiations. (2) Regarding the relocation issue, it is planned to be resolved immediately. Regarding the issue of selling existing houses and real estate, if there is a solution, a new county will be built in the Beiqiao area in the future to prepare for relocation. After the report, the discussion began, and the instrument resolution, (1) the county chief submitted the bill to the second and third district chiefs, requesting an appropriation of funds for the treatment of meningitis inflammation, how to raise the case, and it was decided that the prevention funds should be borne by Shanghai Hospital, the Education Bureau, and the district office each with one third. (2) The county chief submitted the bill to the second district chief, requesting a clear order to abolish the title of Tudong, justice how should the case be handled, and it was decided that the county government would issue a notice on April 1 to be abolished at the same time as the Dibao. (3) The county chief submitted the bill on how to carry out the county's literacy campaign. It was decided that the Education Bureau would formulate detailed measures for the movement propaganda week. (4) The fourth district chief suggested that the special municipal police detectives should handle the arrest of criminals in the county together with the county public security bureau. It was decided that the county should send a letter to the municipal government to instruct the municipal public security bureau to handle the matter. (5) The county chief submitted the bill, proposing to hold the county's defense conference immediately. It was decided that the county party headquarters, the public security bureau chief, the district chiefs, the heads of the guard groups, the heads of the public security sub-bureaus, the director of the property office, and the chairman of the chamber of commerce would be convened at 2:00 PM on the 27th of this month for a meeting (the notice was issued yesterday). The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

Female Bandit Escapes

At 10:00 PM last night, at the east end of Dongxinqiao Street, Caishijie, in the French Concession, a female bandit grabbed jewelry from a woman riding in a rickshaw. The female bandit, about 20 years old, was standing in the middle of the road in front of the Xie Shunxiang New Clothing Store. A woman riding in a rickshaw was going from west to east. The bandit stopped the car and forcibly grabbed the jewelry. The woman was quick-witted and got out of the car to chase, but the female bandit escaped into Baoxing Lane. She was not arrested.

Fire Report

▲Dong Youheng Road: At 11:57 AM yesterday, a fire broke out at the Japanese-owned Sanwa Yarn Factory in Wuling Lane, Dong Youheng Road, Yalu Road. The Hongkou Fire Brigade immediately drove to the scene after hearing the news. Six out of ten of the entire houses were damaged.

▲Xiamen Road: At around 8:00 PM last night, a fire broke out at No. 422, Xiamen Road. The Central Rescue Association drove to the scene to rescue it, but it had already been extinguished.

Recent News from the Silk and Dyeing Association

The Shanghai Silk Dyeing Industry Labor and Management Jointly Formed Price Dyeing Committee has been actively carrying out price dyeing internally and externally in recent days. All silk shops that have not paid the dye account in the first month will be notified in the newspaper by a lawyer and given a time limit to pay it off. The staff is stepping up its work to prepare for all matters related to collecting accounts in the second month, and is arranging various implementation methods, which are very perfect.

Reorganization of the Tea Industry Branch

The Shanghai Nanshi Tea Industry Branch, which is organized by tea shops throughout the city, has been ordered to reorganize into the Tea Industry Guild. Yesterday, fifteen preparatory committee members were elected. (1) Ring the bell to open the meeting and perform the ceremony as usual. (2) Hu Jizhi was publicly elected to open the ballot box, Yang Shangting inspected the ballots, and Wang Yinting read the ballots. (3) In accordance with the law, Wang Caitang, Yang Shangting, Wang Junchen, and others, fifteen people, were elected as preparatory committee members, and reported to the superior authorities for record in accordance with the reorganization procedures. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Police Detectives Promoted

Police detectives Wang Shunlin, Kang Zengxiang, Geng Debiao, Zhou Honglin, Jiang Jinsen, and Zhang Jinlong of the Public Concession Police Force have been promoted to detectives by the police force for their outstanding performance and repeated achievements to show encouragement.

Wuyuan Fellow Villagers Association Election Results Announced

The Wuyuan Fellow Villagers Association held its third election meeting yesterday, publicly nominating Wang Weiying as representative and Liu Changyan as chairman. The ceremony was conducted according to protocol. The chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting, and the ballot box was opened in public. A total of 157 votes were cast. The elected executive committee members were Yu Langxi, Zhu Fengchi, Wang Weiying, Yu Jianhu, Jiang Meizhong, Zheng Jianyuan, Zhan Shaoting, Yu Chenwu, Wang Boqi, Zhan Fuxi, Wang Yucheng, Cheng Zhenjun, Shan Shouhe, Zhan Dafu, Hong Jianting, Sun Zifu, Hu Jingyun, Li Futian, Zha Liting, Wang Lizhai, Wu Bochao, Yu Zufan, Li Jianxian, Wang Huicheng, Zha Ziyuan, Zhan Qianfu, and Zhan Mingshan. The alternate executive committee members were Jiang Guijian, Jin Huiji, Li Zhifang, Hu Zigao, Zha Zhenhua, Yu Xiji, and Cao Yinfu. The elected supervisory committee members were Shi Keyu, Jiang Youbai, Wu Senrong, Wang Langzhou, Yu Yun Kang, Zhao Wenyuan, Cheng Shaonan, Wang Zhiting, and Shi Zhengmao. The alternate supervisory committee members were Zhan Furen, Yu Ming, and Cao Jixuan. The meeting concluded at dusk.

Lost Girl and Boy Awaiting Claim

The Municipal Public Security Bureau reported that the Second District sent in a lost boy, You Minxin, found at Xinqiao Road. After detailed inquiry, he only stated his name as Dao Mingxin, aged seven. His father is a tailor and his mother is a maid. When asked about his parents' names, address, road name, lane number, and house number, he knew nothing. The child has a long face, shaved head, and a red sore scar on the lowest joint of his right thumb. He wears a black velvet rope hat, a red and checkered lined robe, a light gray lake crepe lined vest, a black striped cotton robe, a tea-green cotton jacket, a white red and green striped cloth shirt, and green striped cotton pants with two square blue striped cloths patched on the knees. He also has red velvet and green silk velvet shoes. He carries a small wooden clip, a green pencil, a floral handkerchief, and a stamped iron leaf. The Fourth District also sent in a lost woman, Wang Zhoushi. She stated that she is 22 years old, from Tongzhou, and her husband's name is Zhao Hua, who earns a living by pushing a cart, and she does not know the address. The woman wears a blue satin drill cotton jacket, small red floral foreign cloth pants, white foreign thread socks, and black satin shoes. The Second District also sent in a lost girl. She stated that her name is A Zhao, aged seven. When asked about her parents' names and address, she knew nothing. The child has paralysis in both feet, wears a green lined jacket and striped cloth pants, and foreign thread socks and cotton shoes. All of the above have been sent to the Xin Puyu Hall for care and are awaiting claim.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather was changing, but there would not be rain. North of the Taiwan Strait, a gentle breeze came from the southeast. To the south, the wind was light and without direction. There was fog between Fujian and Shandong. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in the city was 75.0 and the lowest was 50.2. On the same day last year, the highest was 73.4 and the lowest was 57.9.

Letter to the Editor

Regarding the news item in your newspaper's local news column, [Investigation Reveals Reactionary Suspicions in Zhonggong Student Theft Case], which is inconsistent with the facts. The Wusong Seventh District Office came to our school on the 20th because a student had lost money, and they sent personnel to investigate. Several seals were found in student Deng Zhongbang's box. It has now been clarified that they were deposited by Huang Yao, a graduate of our school from the previous academic year. There is a Fudan Summer School certificate submitted by Huang Yao to the Academic Affairs Office as proof. The words engraved on the seals, [Socialism], [Famous Learning], [Chinese Economic Issues], etc., are all course titles and have no reactionary implications. Furthermore, since these seals were forged by Huang Yao, our school has already severely investigated the matter. As for the section in your newspaper stating that District Officer Li's testimony has reactionary implications, this is completely untrue. We hereby request that you make corrections. To the News Department of Shen Bao, Secretariat of China Public School, March 24.

Business News

▲ Depositors' Group Visits Underwear Factory The China ABC Underwear Weaving Factory announced that since the factory added 300 new electric weaving machines and greatly expanded, it did not issue shares, but established a bonus share savings department, allowing people to invest. This has become a solid industry. To strengthen its credit, the factory invited a group of major depositors, including Shen Zaiting, Li Qingxiang, Zhang Zhaotang, Gu Yuequan, Luo Yuxiao, Xu Yongqing, Zhang Feipeng, Luo Risheng, Gu Weichuan, Huang Li, Yuan Xun'an, Ye Renhao, Yao Fengzhen, Guo Jianxiao, Guan Shiquan, Rong Dafang, Qin Guiqing, and dozens of others, in five cars to visit the factory on Kang Nai Tuo Road at 2:00 PM yesterday. General Manager Huang Hongjun personally received them and led them into the tailoring, sewing, weaving, warp, weft, sizing, and ironing departments, explaining everything in detail. They all praised the agility of the machines, the proper arrangement, and the successful completion of the sawtooth-style new cloth factory, which covers more than ten acres and is fully lit. Connected to the old factory, the 350 weaving machines are arranged, each with a motor, without the use of belt drives, saving a lot of money each year. The workers are quick and efficient, which shows that Mr. Huang's supervision is effective and the factory is developing well, which is not accidental. The visit ended at 4:00 PM.

▲ Guanshengyuan Expansion Section to Open Tomorrow The Nanjing Road Guanshengyuan Food Company announced that the main store's business has been developing rapidly recently, especially the attached Guanqi Photography Department, which has made great strides. A month ago, the left-side storefront was renovated to expand business. This project has been completed, and preparations are being actively made to add photography materials and electric engraved silverware departments. It is scheduled to officially open tomorrow and will offer a big sale for 14 days. During the sale period, those who take photos in the department will receive a 50% discount on the original price.

▲ French Baoduo Foreign Firm Hosts Banquet The French Baoduo Foreign Firm at 39 Aiduya Road announced that the firm has been established for many years and specializes in import and export of various goods. It has its own woolen, silk, and wine factories in France, with strong capital and excellent credit. The goods handled are of high quality and low price, so business is exceptionally prosperous. This spring, Mr. Wu Sudan and Mr. Sun Yangnong were newly hired as Chinese managers. The two gentlemen are giants in the business world, with extensive social connections and sufficient experience. The business prospects are expected to improve rapidly. Recently (on the 22nd), the firm hosted a banquet for various circles at Xinghualou on Sima Road. The firm's general manager, Mr. Di Pihe (who is currently the chairman of the Shanghai French Chamber of Commerce and a director of the French Concession), the export department manager, Mr. Mai Ya, and Mr. Wu and Mr. Sun personally received the guests. The guests were all prominent figures in the business world, gathering together in a grand occasion.

▲ Puyi Real Estate Monthly Published The Puyi Real Estate Company announced that the company's business is developing and that it made a lot of profit last year, due to its excellent credit and good service. The company's March real estate monthly publication combines Chinese and Western writing, detailing current silver market land prices, etc. It also contributes to the resolution of disputes between landlords and tenants. Those interested in real estate can write to the company at 50 Nanjing Road to request a copy.

Business News

▲ Samsung Factory's Domestic Pure Wool Serge The Nanjing Road Samsung Cotton and Iron Factory announced that the spring big sale of its Dian Guang brand products at the general distribution office is especially cheap. Recently, it has also launched domestic pure wool serge and overcoat fabrics, which are pioneers in resisting foreign goods. They are most suitable for making Zhongshan suits, student uniforms, and overcoats. Recently, purchases by institutions and schools have been very crowded.

▲ Huazhang Hosts Banquet for Yunsha Wholesale Merchants The Henan Road Huazhang Store announced that the store has been established for more than 60 years and is a famous old store. It has built a large factory in Guangdong, specializing in weaving new floral yunsha and kaochou fabrics. It personally supervises dyeing, sunning, and kao processing. The products are of excellent quality, washable, and durable, and are well-received by society. Therefore, every year goods are shipped from Guangdong to Shanghai and sell well in various places, especially wholesale. Now new goods have arrived one after another, and a special banquet was held last night at Xinghualou on Sima Road for north and south wholesale merchants, with more than 300 people attending, which was a grand occasion.

▲ YMCA Western Restaurant Improves Cuisine The YMCA Western Restaurant announced that starting from the 15th of this month, the restaurant has reorganized all the dishes and specially improved them. The cooking strives for exquisite taste and is suitable for the palate. In recent days, it has been praised by ladies from all walks of life. The director is therefore even more motivated to supervise the chefs to enforce cleanliness. The prices are also very reasonable. Company main dishes are available in three types: $1.20, $0.90, and $0.70 per serving. Electric furnace Bang Ge Lian coffee is $0.20 per serving. Various American biscuits and candies are also sold at prices cheaper than the public.

▲ Shengda Envelope Factory Relocates The Shengda Factory announced that the factory has always been famous for its cheap and beautiful machine-made envelopes. Now, because the distribution office is rebuilding its house, it has moved to Lane 2, Baokangli, north of Beijing Road on Zhejiang Road. Business is as usual. The paper for the produced stationery envelopes, both Chinese and Western paper, various sizes, single-layer and multi-layer, are all fully available. Requesting a full set of samples only requires four cents of postage, so that various sectors can make comparisons in advance, which shows credibility. Major companies, businesses, and institutions in this city and other places are now eagerly buying and printing them.

▲ Yulun's Business is Wildly Popular The Yulun Silk and Satin Store, west of the Nanjing Road Ball Court, announced that since the store opened, business has been very prosperous. It pioneered weekly discount prices, which has never been done in the silk and satin industry. During the third weekly discount period after the opening, there were crowds of people, scrambling to buy. They all said that the various goods are not only new and pleasing in design, but also fairly priced. In addition, the weekly discounts give an extra 11% off the marked price, so the price is half a yuan cheaper per foot than the market price.

Theater News

▲ Wuchang Grand Theater Screens The Ten Commandments The Wuchang Grand Theater announced that Paramount Pictures' famous production, the masterpiece The Ten Commandments by the great director Cecil B. DeMille, is a name known to almost everyone who has seen movies. The Grand Theater is now responding to requests from all walks of life and has rented it for screening. The film must be sent to other places soon and will only be shown at the theater today and tomorrow.

▲ Kadete Asks Han Langen to Perform The Kadete Theater announced that Mr. Han Langen is a famous comedy doctor, whose invented dances, newly composed songs, and jokes are extremely rich. All those who watch them burst out laughing. Recently, there has also been the organization of the Small Eight Entertainment Association, whose programs are colorful and bizarre. The program includes Ge Ge I Love You, Wang Lianying's dance performance, Zhang Jiaxiang's dance, and Ningbo Mei Lanfang's Siming Opera. When the Qing Tian Company's production A Hundred Tribulations of Love was screened at the Zhonghua Grand Theater some time ago, Mr. Han was invited to perform on stage, and the results were excellent, with full houses every day. Starting today, the theater will also screen the film and will continue to invite Mr. Han to perform his latest original Small Entertainment Association day and night to entertain the audience. Prices remain the same to show preferential treatment.

▲ Broken Piano Building Ticket Sales Break New Record The Mingxing Film Company announced that its new film Broken Piano Building is director Zheng Zhengqiu's most proud work and one of the most brilliant performances by Ms. Hu Die since she entered the film industry. Other talents are also rich in screen experience, concentrating and actively cooperating. This film, based on a famous novel, is truly the most valuable masterpiece since domestic films have existed. The film has been screened at the Central since last Saturday, with comedy performances by Mr. Zheng, Ms. Hu, and others on stage. Since the opening, every show has been sold out, and there have been many viewers who regretted missing out. The Central's ticket sales record is headed by this film. From the 25th, it has moved to the New Central Theater for screening.

Publishing News

▲ Postal Studies Monthly Improved The Postal Studies Monthly, Volumes 2, Issues 4 and 5, has been published. There is a declaration stating that the monthly publication after publication will not only transmit news and report news, but will continue postal rides and conduct specialized postal research. Therefore, in the future, all unfinished masterpieces in postal rides, such as the Chinese Postal National Mirror, etc., will be gradually completed in the monthly publication. Therefore, the monthly publication is a microcosm of postal rides. All those who previously subscribed to postal rides should quickly subscribe to the monthly publication, otherwise they will be incomplete, because any manuscript that has already appeared in the monthly publication will no longer be disclosed in future postal rides. The selling price remains the same at 10 cents per copy. Distribution locations: Commercial Press on Chessboard Street, Civilization Bookstore on Daimalu.

Astrology News

▲ Xie Youshi Arrives in Shanghai Xie Youshi of Beiping announced that I have been in the military and political circles for many years. In view of the turmoil in the officialdom, I have come to Shanghai to make a living by fortune-telling. I have set up my desk at the Yuanhao branch of the Pingjiang New Hotel on Daxin Street. Those who have heard of my name come in droves. My words are pertinent and free from worldly habits. In all other respects, I am truly a unique figure in the world of prophecy.
